def excel_SUM(*args):
    vals = []
    for a in args:
        if isinstance(a, (list, tuple)):
            vals.extend(a)
        else:
            vals.append(a)
    return sum(v for v in vals if v is not None)

def excel_MIN(*args):
    vals = []
    for a in args:
        if isinstance(a, (list, tuple)):
            vals.extend(a)
        else:
            vals.append(a)
    return min((v for v in vals if v is not None), default=None)

def excel_MAX(*args):
    vals = []
    for a in args:
        if isinstance(a, (list, tuple)):
            vals.extend(a)
        else:
            vals.append(a)
    return max((v for v in vals if v is not None), default=None)

def excel_AVERAGE(*args):
    vals = []
    for a in args:
        if isinstance(a, (list, tuple)):
            vals.extend(a)
        else:
            vals.append(a)
    vals = [v for v in vals if v is not None]
    return sum(vals) / len(vals) if vals else None

def excel_IF(cond, val_true, val_false):
    return val_true if cond else val_false

def excel_POWER(x, y):
    return x ** y

def excel_AND(*args):
    return all(args)

def excel_OR(*args):
    return any(args)

def excel_NOT(val):
    return not val

def excel_ABS(val):
    return abs(val)

def excel_ROUND(val, ndigits=0):
    return round(val, int(ndigits))

def excel_CEILING(val, significance=1):
    import math
    return math.ceil(val / significance) * significance

def excel_FLOOR(val, significance=1):
    import math
    return math.floor(val / significance) * significance

def excel_MOD(a, b):
    return a % b

def excel_SQRT(val):
    import math
    return math.sqrt(val)

def excel_EXP(val):
    import math
    return math.exp(val)

def excel_LOG(val, base=10):
    import math
    return math.log(val, base)

def excel_LOG10(val):
    import math
    return math.log10(val)

def excel_TRUNC(val, ndigits=0):
    import math
    factor = 10.0 ** int(ndigits)
    return math.trunc(val * factor) / factor

def excel_SIGN(val):
    return (val > 0) - (val < 0)

def excel_CONCAT(*args):
    return ''.join(str(a) for a in args if a is not None)

def excel_LEFT(text, num_chars):
    return str(text)[:int(num_chars)]

def excel_RIGHT(text, num_chars):
    return str(text)[-int(num_chars):]

def excel_MID(text, start, num_chars):
    return str(text)[int(start)-1:int(start)-1+int(num_chars)]

def excel_LEN(text):
    return len(str(text))

def excel_FIND(find_text, within_text, start=1):
    try:
        return str(within_text).index(str(find_text), int(start)-1) + 1
    except ValueError:
        return 0

def excel_SEARCH(find_text, within_text, start=1):
    try:
        return str(within_text).lower().index(str(find_text).lower(), int(start)-1) + 1
    except ValueError:
        return 0

def excel_REPLACE(old_text, start, num_chars, new_text):
    old_text = str(old_text)
    start = int(start) - 1
    num_chars = int(num_chars)
    return old_text[:start] + str(new_text) + old_text[start+num_chars:]

def excel_UPPER(text):
    return str(text).upper()

def excel_LOWER(text):
    return str(text).lower()

def excel_PROPER(text):
    return str(text).title()

def excel_VALUE(text):
    try:
        return float(text)
    except:
        return None

def excel_NOW():
    from datetime import datetime
    return datetime.now()

def excel_TODAY():
    from datetime import datetime
    return datetime.today().date()

def excel_DATE(year, month, day):
    from datetime import date
    return date(int(year), int(month), int(day))

def excel_YEAR(date_val):
    return date_val.year

def excel_MONTH(date_val):
    return date_val.month

def excel_DAY(date_val):
    return date_val.day

def excel_HOUR(date_val):
    return date_val.hour

def excel_MINUTE(date_val):
    return date_val.minute

def excel_SECOND(date_val):
    return date_val.second

def excel_DATEDIF(start_date, end_date, unit):
    from datetime import datetime
    d1 = start_date if not isinstance(start_date, str) else datetime.strptime(start_date, "%Y-%m-%d")
    d2 = end_date if not isinstance(end_date, str) else datetime.strptime(end_date, "%Y-%m-%d")
    if unit == "Y":
        return d2.year - d1.year - ((d2.month, d2.day) < (d1.month, d1.day))
    elif unit == "M":
        return (d2.year - d1.year) * 12 + d2.month - d1.month - (d2.day < d1.day)
    elif unit == "D":
        return (d2 - d1).days
    else:
        return None

def excel_VLOOKUP(lookup_value, table, col_index, exact=True):
    for row in table:
        if (row[0] == lookup_value) if exact else (str(lookup_value) in str(row[0])):
            return row[col_index-1]
    return None

def excel_HLOOKUP(lookup_value, table, row_index, exact=True):
    if not table or not table[0]:
        return None
    for idx, val in enumerate(table[0]):
        if (val == lookup_value) if exact else (str(lookup_value) in str(val)):
            return table[row_index-1][idx]
    return None

def excel_INDEX(array, row_num, col_num):
    return array[row_num-1][col_num-1]

def excel_MATCH(lookup_value, array, match_type=0):
    if match_type == 0:
        for idx, val in enumerate(array):
            if val == lookup_value:
                return idx + 1
    elif match_type == 1:
        for idx, val in enumerate(array):
            if val > lookup_value:
                return idx
        return len(array)
    elif match_type == -1:
        for idx, val in enumerate(array):
            if val < lookup_value:
                return idx
        return len(array)
    return None

def excel_ISNUMBER(val):
    try:
        float(val)
        return True
    except:
        return False

def excel_ISBLANK(val):
    return val is None or (isinstance(val, str) and val.strip() == "")

def excel_ISERROR(val):
    try:
        return isinstance(val, Exception)
    except:
        return True

def excel_N(val):
    if isinstance(val, (int, float)):
        return val
    return 0

def excel_TEXT(val, format_text):
    try:
        return format(val, format_text)
    except:
        return str(val)

def excel_IFERROR(expr, alt_value):
    try:
        return expr
    except Exception:
        return alt_value

def excel_IFS(*args):
    for i in range(0, len(args) - 1, 2):
        if args[i]:
            return args[i + 1]
    if len(args) % 2 == 1:
        return args[-1]
    return None

def excel_RIGHT(text, num_chars):
    return str(text)[-int(num_chars):]
